posted:Posted March 17, 2024
msg:A perfect experience!
We checked in on the first night. The two front desk staff were professional and efficient. They provided smiling service throughout the whole process, which made us feel at home after a day of wind in Wanlong on Saturday. What was rare was that we were upgraded to a twin room on the 5th floor facing the ski resort. Considering that we would return to Beijing at 1:30 pm after skiing, they thoughtfully checked out for us at 2:00 pm. Thank you. The children commented that it was worthy of being a star hotel.
The hotel is newly built, and the room facilities are very new. There is a large bathtub in the room. There is no better experience than taking a hot bath after struggling on the ski slope for a day! The room temperature is very high, but fortunately a humidifier is provided so that it is not too dry. The room has an unbeatable view. You can see A and B ropes below, and you can see the ski slopes strung together by Leo and Virgo in the distance.
The breakfast is very rich, and the waiter is polite and asked us in a low voice if we want tea or coffee.
The hotel can ski in and out. After applying for the ski ticket on the 1st floor, you can go out to B rope. Although it is not as big as the ski resort lobby on the Zhixuan side, it is only for guests, small and efficient. We saw a row of snowboards at the exit, probably stored by the tenants, we didn't use them.
This weekend we took our kids on a snowboard trip, Yunzhen and Yinhe Ski Resort left us with wonderful memories of the 23-24 snow season. Let's fight again at Cuiyun Mountain Yinhe in the next snow season!

msg:I came here for skiing, and I am so satisfied with this hotel! The hotel is grand and new! The room is big enough, and the ski resort is downstairs, you can ski in and out, and you can go back to the room to lie down and continue skiing when you are tired. The service is also very good. The clothes and snowshoes and snowboards provided by the ski resort are all SALOMON, very new. Because there are too few people for breakfast, we can't open a buffet, so we changed to a la carte, which is a better experience. I feel that this Cuiyun Mountain Ski Resort is very suitable for beginners to advance. There is a Virgo ski slope, which is very friendly to beginners like me who have just learned to change edges and are not good at changing edges. The distance is long enough, about 2km, the slope is gentle enough, there are few people, and the snow quality is also good. It kills all the ski resorts in Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Shanghai. Skiing for a day can get rapid advancement! The only disadvantage is that the ski resort is on the sunny side, so it basically has to be closed in March, because the snow melts during the day and it is all ice at night, so it is impossible to ski at night. Fulong and Wanlong are both on the shady side, and it is estimated that they can be open until April. I can only say that you must ski in the north to find real happiness, and you must come every year in the future!

I am very happy to have chosen Yunzhen Jinling Cuiyun Mountain Hotel. We were a few of us with families. We chose Yunzhen at that time because it was close to the track and we could walk directly from the hotel to the track, which was more convenient. After checking in, the perfect hotel service made us affirm this choice.
The hotel room is very large, with sufficient heating and a balcony facing the snow track. It is very satisfying to get up early and watch the sun shine on the snow track. I must thank the customer service Pei Mengmeng here for helping to book and arrange the room. She is patient and professional. If you have any questions about skiing, just consult her. Attached is the mobile phone number **********.
I also want to thank the customer service manager Zhao Yufeng. In addition to the ski tickets, the hotel also comes with a ticket to the Snow Park. It takes less than ten minutes to walk there. It is worth a visit. The facilities in the field are a bit old, but the thick snow itself is full of fun. The only regret is that our schedule was too tight and we couldn't take the cable car to the mountaintop library. name:Z‚Äçu‚Äçi‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçf‚Äçu‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçm‚Äçi‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg

posted:Posted December 24, 2023
msg:Cuiyunshan Ski Resort is right next to the hotel. There are not many people skiing on weekdays. The intermediate trails are okay. The ski equipment hall is on the first floor. It is super convenient to slide in and out. The ski equipment is relatively new and the snowboards are not very old. very good! The one-day ticket (including ski equipment + cable car) is 399 yuan, which is not expensive. It costs 100 yuan to go up to the cable car alone (it cannot be repeated and can only go up once). There is a cafe and library on the top of the mountain that is worth visiting.
The hotel service is very good, which is the biggest advantage. The reserved executive twin room was upgraded to an executive suite for free, with a better view, facing Cuiyun Mountain-Yinhe Ski Resort! Floor manager: Nan Yaping, who greets us cordially every day and meets our needs in a timely manner, such as replenishing capsule coffee at any time, repairing bedroom lights, providing disposable bathtub bath masks, etc.
The room facilities are very complete, including a welcome fruit plate and welcome drink. A humidifier is provided, and toiletries are from Herborist. The sound insulation is good, it's very close to the elevator and it's not noisy at all. The balcony is large and has a wide view, but it's too cold (the highest temperature is -26 degrees) to stay outside. We came here for Chris**as in mid-December, and Chongli was really cold!
The catering is not bad, and the breakfast restaurant offers Hebei specialties: mutton soup, bacon flatbread, Hebei fried dough, salty porridge, etc., as well as Chinese delicacies such as tofu brain fried dough sticks. I am used to eating Western breakfast. Coffee, milk, whole wheat bread and omelets are also available (not many varieties), and there are not many vegetable salads and fruits. The Chinese breakfast is obviously more comprehensive.
Dinner at the Japanese restaurant on the second floor was very good. The hot ramen, grilled bird skewers, and side dishes were all very good! However, I have also eaten at the Chinese restaurant on the 9th floor. It was average. The dishes, noodles and rice were too greasy.
The transportation is convenient. The hotel is not far from the Jingli Expressway. The GPS is easy to find. Parking goes directly to the basement. Hotel guests park for free for a few days. It is very good because there is no need to defrost due to snow.
Overall, I am very satisfied. Compared with other ski hotels I have stayed in such as Wanlong, Fulong and Taiwu, it is indeed good. I will come back in the future.
